## RPCs According to Builds and Installs of 999
    
There are __432 (4.17%)__ builds defining __3,277__ RPCs distributed from _1996-05-24_ to _2017-10-24_, __248 (57.41%)__ of which introduce new RPCs. RPC _PSB USERLOAD_ appears in the most builds, __9__. The median number of RPCs per Build is __1.0__. 

RPCs are spread across __62__ packages. Package _ORDER ENTRY/RESULTS REPORTING_ has the most RPCs, __1,008__. __20__ RPCs have more than one Package usually because of re-organization and splitting of Packages over the years. __2__ RPCs have no package because their builds weren't assigned a package (yet).

Builds can delete as well as add RPCs - __69__ of the RPCs were deleted by the final Build they appeared in, leaving __3,208__ RPCs active and installed.

File _8994_ is suppossed to define the active RPCs in a VistA. However the 8994 of this system has __0__ deleted RPCs, is missing __3__ active RPCs and has __471__ extra RPCs that never appear in a Build.
    
61 Packages have RPCs, while 2 RPCs have no Package. Clearly the top Packages (ORDERS, IMAGES and some COTS packages) need to be examined first ...
